      <!--推荐理由-->
      <dd class="last">
       <div class="tt">
        <h1>
         推荐理由：
        </h1>
       </div>
       <a class="reason">
        TAWNY(茶色)波特：也称为“陈年波特”，是比较温和精细的木桶陈化酒,比宝石波特存放在木桶里的时间要长,一直在木桶里要等到出现茶色（一般指的是红茶色）。茶色波特一般有着好闻的干果香，适合于做餐后甜点酒。优质意大利葡萄酒，红色恋曲，口感清新，待着明亮的酸度，较低的单宁带有一点点干涩，附带着黑色的水果的清香，很适合初级红酒入门者。
       </a>
      </dd>
     </dl>

   $(document).ready(function () {
        $(document).delegate("#getnextPage", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike($('#getnextPage').attr('flash').toString(),'add');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#sh", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('SH','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#pp", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('PP','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#cj", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('CJ','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#fs", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('FS','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#sw", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('SW','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#bg", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('BG','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#ym", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('YM','no');
        });
        $(document).delegate("#yz", "click", function () {
            guessYourLike('YZ','no');
        });

        //页面初始化
        guessYourLike('SH');
    });

    function guessYourLike(type,flag){
        $('#getnextPage').attr("flash",type);
        //alert("type="+type);
        var page = $('#guessPageNum').attr('page');
        if (flag=='no' || page==null || ++page > 5) {
            page = 1;
        }
        YM.dataproxy.ajax({
            url: "/index6/guessYourLike.jspa?time="+(new Date()).getTime(),
            data: {pageNum: page,type:type},
            dataType: 'text',
            success: function (data) {
                var tt = $('#guessPageNum').parent();
                tt.children('#guessPageNum').remove();
                tt.append(data);
            }
        });
    }

    /**

            data: "goodsId="+goodsId,
            dataType : 'json',
            success: function(json){
                //alert("msg="+json.msg);
            }
        });
    }

	var d = document.createElement('script');
	d.src=url+'&rand='+Math.random();
	var s = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
	s.parentNode.insertBefore(d, s);
};
	if (YM.cookie.get('keyname')=='brd'){

		if (window.location.search.getQueryValue('utm_source')=='brd'){ // landingPage

			loadJs('https://aw.kejet.net/t?p=Tvb&c=j2');

});

  <script>
   showChooseMemberWin = function (data) {
        var $win = $('#sitesSelector').window({
            title: "<span class='bgwhite'>账号合并</span>",
            width: 800,
            height: 450,
            top: '20%',
            left: '50%',
            shadow: true,
            modal: true,
//            iconCls: 'icon-add',
            closed: true,
            minimizable: false,
            maximizable: false,
            collapsible: false
        });
        $win.window('open');
        $('#sitesSelector').show();
        loadData(data);
    }

    function loadData(data) {
        $("#sitePanel").find("tbody").append(data);
    }


    function chooseMainMemeber() {
        if($("input[name='chooseMainMember']:checked").size()==0){
            YM.page.alert("请先选择主账号!");
        }
        else {
            var id=$("input[name='chooseMainMember']:checked").attr("id").substr(3);
            YM.page.confirm("确定将编号为"+id+"的账号申请为主账号？",function () {
                var bindMemberIds=[];
                $.each($("input[name='chooseMainMember']"),function (index,item) {
                    bindMemberIds.push($(item).attr("id").substr(3));
                });

                var pm={
                    bindMainMemberId:id,
                    bindMemberIds:bindMemberIds
                };

                $.post("/personalCenter/bindApply.jspa",pm,function (data) {
                    YM.page.alert(data.msg);
                    if(data.applyStatus) {//申请成功,手机号码已经在申请中了
                        setTimeout(function () {
                            window.location.href = "//www.yesmywine.com";
                        }, 500);
                    }
                },"json");
            });
        }

    }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function () {
        //绑定手机号
        setTimeout(function () {
            doBindMobile();
        },1200);


    });

    //查询如果此账号没有绑定手机，则弹出绑定手机号框
    //0未绑定手机号 1 绑定了一个手机号  2 绑定了多个手机号  3 未登录
    function doBindMobile() {
        //return;
        $.get("/userCenter/checkMobileStatus.jspa",{},function (data) {
            if("3"==data||"1"==data){
            }
            else if("0"==data){
               //弹出绑定手机的页面
               BIND.page.member.setAccountSecurity('绑定手机','bindMobile');
           }
           else{
               showChooseMemberWin(data);
           }
        });

    }

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var shtml = "";
	shtml += '<div style="width:100%;">'
	shtml += '<a href="http://www.baidu.com"  style="width:90%;margin:0% 5%;display:block;text-align:center;">';
	shtml += '    <img style="border-radius:20px" id="maskImg" src=""/>';
	shtml += '</a>';
	shtml += '<span style="width:50px;height:50px;display:block;background:url(images/close.png) top center no-repeat;background-size:100% 100%;margin:6% auto 0;" onclick="maskClose();"></span>';
	shtml += '</div>'
	var masks = $('<div class="mask"  style="position:fixed;top:0;left:0;z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,.5);"></div>');
	$('body').append(masks);
	masks.html(shtml);
	masks.hide();
	
	var map = new BMap.Map("container");
	var point = new BMap.Point(116.331398, 39.897445);
	var myCity = new BMap.LocalCity();
	var cityCode;
	var cityName;
	map.centerAndZoom(point, 12);
	myCity.get(myFun);

	function myFun(result) {
		cityName = result.name;
		map.setCenter(cityName);
		cityCode = result.code;
//		if(cityName.indexOf('北京') == 0 || cityName.indexOf('武汉') == 0 ){
		mask(cityCode);
//		}
	}
	function mask(cityCode){
		$.ajax({
			type:"post",
			url:"/index/getpopupurl.jspa",
			dataType:'json',
//			jsonpCallback:'callback',
			async:false,
			data:{
				cityCode:cityCode
//				difDomain:true
			},
			success:function(res){
				if(res.flag == 1){
					var data = res.data;
					var shows = function() {
						$('.mask').show();
					}
					browserRedirect(data); //判断设备
					imgLode("maskImg", shows);
				}else{
					
				}
			}
		});
	}
	//弹屏关闭
	function maskClose(){
		$('.mask').hide();
	}
	//判断图片是否加载完成，完成执行回调函数
	function imgLode(imgId,callback){
		var callback = callback;
		document.getElementById(imgId).onload = function(e){
			e.stopPropagation();
			callback();
		}
	}
	//判断设备：移动还是pc
	function browserRedirect(data) {
        var sUserAgent = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        var bIsIpad = sUserAgent.match(/ipad/i) == "ipad";
        var bIsIphoneOs = sUserAgent.match(/iphone os/i) == "iphone os";
        var bIsMidp = sUserAgent.match(/midp/i) == "midp";
        var bIsUc7 = sUserAgent.match(/rv:1.2.3.4/i) == "rv:1.2.3.4";
        var bIsUc = sUserAgent.match(/ucweb/i) == "ucweb";
        var bIsAndroid = sUserAgent.match(/android/i) == "android";
        var bIsCE = sUserAgent.match(/windows ce/i) == "windows ce";
        var bIsWM = sUserAgent.match(/windows mobile/i) == "windows mobile";
        if (bIsIpad || bIsIphoneOs || bIsMidp || bIsUc7 || bIsUc || bIsAndroid || bIsCE || bIsWM) {
            $('.mask a #maskImg').css('width','100%');
			$('.mask a img').attr('src',data.popupImgUrl);
			$('.mask a').attr('href', data.popupUrl + '?mchType=1&cityCode='+ cityCode +'&cityName='+ cityName+'&gdymwapp=ymw');
        } else {
        	$('.mask span').css({
            	'position':'absolute',
            	'top':'-5%',
            	'right':'25%'
            });
            $('.mask a #maskImg').css('width','40%');
			$('.mask a img').attr('src',data.popupPcImgUrl);
			$('.mask a').attr('href', data.popupPcUrl + '?mchType=0&cityCode='+ cityCode +'&cityName='+ cityName+'&gdymwapp=ymw');
        }
    }
  </script>
